Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: piano\\ \tt RIGHT: hand saw\\ \tt TOP: tulip\\ \tt BOTTOM: ruler\\ \tt CENTER: aluminium\\ \tt NORTHWEST: carnation\\ \tt NORTHEAST: highlighter\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: blush\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: lyre\\ \tt HERE: jeans skirt\\ \tt THERE: blueberry\\ \tt NOWHERE: eye shadow\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: flip-flops\\ \tt INSIDE: hiking boots\\ \tt OUTSIDE: post-it notes\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   }
